# Cross-Compiler Sanitizer Tracing: ASan in LLVM vs GCC

## Your Task

AddressSanitizer (ASan) is implemented in both LLVM and GCC. Find the key source files that implement ASan instrumentation in each compiler. In `llvm/llvm-project`: 1. The C++ source file under `compiler-rt/lib/asan/` that implements ASan interceptors for standard library functions. 2. The C++ source file under `compiler-rt/lib/asan/` that implements the ASan runtime initialization. 3. The LLVM pass that inserts ASan instrumentation at the IR level (look for `AddressSanitizer` in `llvm/lib/Transforms/Instrumentation/`). In `gcc-mirror/gcc`: 4. The C++ source file that implements ASan instrumentation in GCC (`gcc/asan.cc`). 5. The header file for ASan in GCC (`gcc/asan.h`). Report the repo, file path, and primary class or function name for each file.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the crossrepo tracing domain.

## Available Resources

No local repositories are pre-checked out.

**Note:** Additional repositories are accessible via Sourcegraph MCP tools:
- `github.com/llvm/llvm-project` (llvm/llvm-project)
- `github.com/gcc-mirror/gcc` (gcc-mirror/gcc)

## Output Format

Create a file at `/workspace/answer.json` with your findings in the following structure:

```json
{
  "files": [
    {"repo": "org/repo-name", "path": "relative/path/to/file.go"}
  ],
  "symbols": [
    {"repo": "org/repo-name", "path": "relative/path/to/file.go", "symbol": "SymbolName"}

}
```

Include only the fields relevant to this task. Your answer is evaluated against a closed-world oracle — completeness matters.

## Summary

The file `/workspace/answer.json` contains:

### LLVM Implementation (github.com/sg-evals/llvm-project--a8f3c97d):

1. **`compiler-rt/lib/asan/asan_interceptors.cpp`** - Implements ASan interceptors for standard library functions using `INTERCEPTOR` macros to wrap libc functions.

2. **`compiler-rt/lib/asan/asan_rtl.cpp`** - Contains the `AsanInitializer` class that handles runtime initialization of ASan, including critical functions for poisoning/unpoisoning memory.

3. **`llvm/lib/Transforms/Instrumentation/AddressSanitizer.cpp`** - Implements the LLVM IR-level instrumentation pass with:
   - `AddressSanitizer` struct - core instrumentation logic
   - `AddressSanitizerPass` class - main LLVM pass interface
   - `ModuleAddressSanitizer` class - module-level instrumentation

### GCC Implementation (github.com/sg-evals/gcc--96dfb333):

4. **`gcc/asan.cc`** - Implements ASan instrumentation with:
   - `asan_finish_file()` function - finalizes ASan processing and registers globals
   - `asan_redzone_buffer` class - manages shadow byte emission for red zones

5. **`gcc/asan.h`** - Header file with:
   - Function declarations
   - Macro definitions (`ASAN_SHADOW_SHIFT`, `ASAN_RED_ZONE_SIZE`, magic numbers)

The answer includes complete file paths, primary classes/functions, and a detailed narrative explaining how each component contributes to ASan's implementation in both compilers.
